<pr_description>
TriggerUtils.ComputeFireTimesBetween does not handle DST properly
Hi,
I think I found a problem with the generation of the fire times when crossing the DST date.
I can reproduce it on the 3.2.4 with .NET 4.7.2.

```
 DateTime startDateTime = new DateTime(2020, 10, 25);
            DateTimeOffset startDateTimeOffset = new DateTimeOffset(startDateTime);
            int daysAhead = 3;

            TriggerBuilder triggerBuilder = TriggerBuilder.Create()
                .WithIdentity("id")
                .ForJob("job")
                .StartAt(new DateTimeOffset(startDateTime.AddMinutes(1).AddSeconds(5)))
                .WithDailyTimeIntervalSchedule(
                    scheduleBuilder =>
                    {
                        scheduleBuilder.OnEveryDay().WithIntervalInHours(24);
                        scheduleBuilder
                            .StartingDailyAt(new TimeOfDay(0, 1, 5))
                            .EndingDailyAt(new TimeOfDay(23, 59, 59))
                            .WithMisfireHandlingInstructionDoNothing();
                    });

            IReadOnlyList<DateTimeOffset> fireTimes =
                TriggerUtils.ComputeFireTimesBetween((
                IOperableTrigger)triggerBuilder.Build(),
                null,
                startDateTimeOffset,
                startDateTimeOffset.AddDays(daysAhead));

            Assert.AreEqual(new DateTimeOffset(new DateTime(2020, 10, 25, 0, 1, 5)), fireTimes.First().LocalDateTime);
            Assert.AreEqual(new DateTimeOffset(new DateTime(2020, 10, 26, 0, 1, 5)), fireTimes.Skip(1).First().LocalDateTime);
            Assert.AreEqual(new DateTimeOffset(new DateTime(2020, 10, 27, 0, 1, 5)), fireTimes.Skip(2).First().LocalDateTime);
```

Expected: According to the setup I would expect 3 dates given in the assert.

Actual: 4 dates, with additional DateTime(2020, 10, 25, 23, 1, 5).


kind regards,
Kamil

</pr_description>

/testbed
     1	#region License
     2	
     3	/*

    21	
    22	using Quartz.Spi;
    23	
    24	namespace Quartz;
    25	
    26	/// <summary>
    27	/// Convenience and utility methods for simplifying the construction and
    28	/// configuration of <see cref="ITrigger" />s and DateTimeOffsetOffsets.
    29	/// </summary>
    30	/// <seealso cref="ICronTrigger" />
    31	/// <seealso cref="ISimpleTrigger" />
    32	/// <author>James House</author>
    33	/// <author>Marko Lahma (.NET)</author>
    34	public static class TriggerUtils
    35	{
    36	    /// <summary>
    37	    /// Returns a list of Dates that are the next fire times of a
    38	    /// <see cref="ITrigger" />.
    39	    /// The input trigger will be cloned before any work is done, so you need
    40	    /// not worry about its state being altered by this method.
    41	    /// </summary>
    42	    /// <param name="trigger">The trigger upon which to do the work</param>
    43	    /// <param name="calendar">The calendar to apply to the trigger's schedule</param>
    44	    /// <param name="numTimes">The number of next fire times to produce</param>
    45	    public static IReadOnlyList<DateTimeOffset> ComputeFireTimes(IOperableTrigger trigger, ICalendar? calendar, int numTimes)
    46	    {
    47	        List<DateTimeOffset> lst = new List<DateTimeOffset>();
    48	
    49	        IOperableTrigger t = (IOperableTrigger) trigger.Clone();
    50	
    51	        if (t.GetNextFireTimeUtc() is null || !t.GetNextFireTimeUtc().HasValue)
    52	        {
    53	            t.ComputeFirstFireTimeUtc(calendar);
    54	        }
    55	
    56	        for (int i = 0; i < numTimes; i++)
    57	        {
    58	            DateTimeOffset? d = t.GetNextFireTimeUtc();
    59	            if (d.HasValue)
    60	            {
    61	                lst.Add(d.Value);
    62	                t.Triggered(calendar);
    63	            }
    64	            else
    65	            {
    66	                break;
    67	            }
    68	        }
    69	
    70	        return lst.AsReadOnly();
    71	    }
    72	
    73	    /// <summary>
    74	    /// Compute the <see cref="DateTimeOffset" /> that is 1 second after the Nth firing of
    75	    /// the given <see cref="ITrigger" />, taking the trigger's associated
    76	    /// <see cref="ICalendar" /> into consideration.
    77	    /// </summary>
    78	    /// <remarks>
    79	    /// The input trigger will be cloned before any work is done, so you need
    80	    /// not worry about its state being altered by this method.
    81	    /// </remarks>
    82	    /// <param name="trigger">The trigger upon which to do the work</param>
    83	    /// <param name="calendar">The calendar to apply to the trigger's schedule</param>
    84	    /// <param name="numberOfTimes">The number of next fire times to produce</param>
    85	    /// <returns>the computed Date, or null if the trigger (as configured) will not fire that many times</returns>
    86	    public static DateTimeOffset? ComputeEndTimeToAllowParticularNumberOfFirings(IOperableTrigger trigger, ICalendar? calendar, int numberOfTimes)
    87	    {
    88	        IOperableTrigger t = (IOperableTrigger) trigger.Clone();
    89	
    90	        if (t.GetNextFireTimeUtc() is null)
    91	        {
    92	            t.ComputeFirstFireTimeUtc(calendar);
    93	        }
    94	
    95	        int c = 0;
    96	        DateTimeOffset? endTime = null;
    97	
    98	        for (int i = 0; i < numberOfTimes; i++)
    99	        {
   100	            DateTimeOffset? d = t.GetNextFireTimeUtc();
   101	            if (d is not null)
   102	            {
   103	                c++;
   104	                t.Triggered(calendar);
   105	                if (c == numberOfTimes)
   106	                {
   107	                    endTime = d;
   108	                }
   109	            }
   110	            else
   111	            {
   112	                break;
   113	            }
   114	        }
   115	
   116	        if (endTime is null)
   117	        {
   118	            return null;
   119	        }
   120	
   121	        endTime = endTime.Value.AddSeconds(1);
   122	
   123	        return endTime;
   124	    }
   125	
   126	
   127	    /// <summary>
   128	    /// Returns a list of Dates that are the next fire times of a  <see cref="ITrigger" />
   129	    /// that fall within the given date range. The input trigger will be cloned
   130	    /// before any work is done, so you need not worry about its state being
   131	    /// altered by this method.
   132	    /// <para>
   133	    /// NOTE: if this is a trigger that has previously fired within the given
   134	    /// date range, then firings which have already occurred will not be listed
   135	    /// in the output List.
   136	    /// </para>
   137	    /// </summary>
   138	    /// <param name="trigger">The trigger upon which to do the work</param>
   139	    /// <param name="calendar">The calendar to apply to the trigger's schedule</param>
   140	    /// <param name="from">The starting date at which to find fire times</param>
   141	    /// <param name="to">The ending date at which to stop finding fire times</param>
   142	    public static IReadOnlyList<DateTimeOffset> ComputeFireTimesBetween(IOperableTrigger trigger, ICalendar? calendar, DateTimeOffset from, DateTimeOffset to)
   143	    {
   144	        List<DateTimeOffset> lst = new List<DateTimeOffset>();
   145	
   146	        IOperableTrigger t = (IOperableTrigger) trigger.Clone();
   147	
   148	        if (t.GetNextFireTimeUtc() is null || !t.GetNextFireTimeUtc().HasValue)
   149	        {
   150	            // Only preserve the trigger's own StartTimeUtc if it falls within
   151	            // the query range [from, to]. This ensures fire times stay aligned
   152	            // with the trigger's configured schedule, while still supporting
   153	            // arbitrary date range queries where from/to define the window.
   154	            if (t.StartTimeUtc < from || t.StartTimeUtc > to)
   155	            {
   156	                t.StartTimeUtc = from;
   157	            }
   158	            if (!t.EndTimeUtc.HasValue || t.EndTimeUtc.Value > to)
   159	            {
   160	                t.EndTimeUtc = to;
   161	            }
   162	            t.ComputeFirstFireTimeUtc(calendar);
   163	        }
   164	
   165	        // TODO: this method could be more efficient by using logic specific
   166	        //        to the type of trigger ...
   167	        while (true)
   168	        {
   169	            DateTimeOffset? d = t.GetNextFireTimeUtc();
   170	            if (d.HasValue)
   171	            {
   172	                if (d.Value < from)
   173	                {
   174	                    t.Triggered(calendar);
   175	                    continue;
   176	                }
   177	                if (d.Value > to)
   178	                {
   179	                    break;
   180	                }
   181	                lst.Add(d.Value);
   182	                t.Triggered(calendar);
   183	            }
   184	            else
   185	            {
   186	                break;
   187	            }
   188	        }
   189	        return lst.AsReadOnly();
   190	    }
   191	}

   659	    /// <summary>
   660	    /// Returns the next time at which the <see cref="IDailyTimeIntervalTrigger" /> will
   661	    /// fire, after the given time. If the trigger will not fire after the given
   662	    /// time, <see langword="null" /> will be returned.
   663	    /// </summary>
   664	    /// <param name="afterTime"></param>
   665	    /// <returns></returns>
   666	    public override DateTimeOffset? GetFireTimeAfter(DateTimeOffset? afterTime)
   667	    {
   668	        // Check if trigger has completed or not.
   669	        if (complete)
   670	        {
   671	            return null;
   672	        }
   673	
   674	        // a. Increment afterTime by a second, so that we are comparing against a time after it!
   675	        if (afterTime is null)
   676	        {
   677	            afterTime = TimeProvider.GetUtcNow().AddSeconds(1);
   678	        }
   679	        else
   680	        {
   681	            afterTime = afterTime.Value.AddSeconds(1);
   682	        }
   683	
   684	        // make sure afterTime is at least startTime
   685	        if (afterTime < startTimeUtc)
   686	        {
   687	            afterTime = startTimeUtc;
   688	        }
   689	
   690	        // now change to local time zone
   691	        afterTime = TimeZoneUtil.ConvertTime(afterTime.Value, TimeZone);
   692	
   693	        // b.Check to see if afterTime is after endTimeOfDay or not.
   694	        // If yes, then we need to advance to next day as well.
   695	        bool afterTimePastEndTimeOfDay = false;
   696	        if (endTimeOfDay is not null)
   697	        {
   698	            afterTimePastEndTimeOfDay = afterTime.Value > endTimeOfDay.GetTimeOfDayForDate(afterTime.Value);
   699	        }
   700	
   701	        // c. now we need to move to the next valid day of week if either:
   702	        // the given time is past the end time of day, or given time is not on a valid day of week
   703	        DateTimeOffset? fireTime = AdvanceToNextDayOfWeekIfNecessary(afterTime.Value, afterTimePastEndTimeOfDay);
   704	
   705	        if (fireTime is null)
   706	        {
   707	            return null;
   708	        }
   709	
   710	        // d. Calculate and save fireTimeEndDate variable for later use
   711	        DateTimeOffset fireTimeEndDate;
   712	        if (endTimeOfDay is null)
   713	        {
   714	            fireTimeEndDate = new TimeOfDay(23, 59, 59).GetTimeOfDayForDate(fireTime.Value);
   715	        }
   716	        else
   717	        {
   718	            fireTimeEndDate = endTimeOfDay.GetTimeOfDayForDate(fireTime.Value);
   719	        }
   720	
   721	        // apply the proper offset for the end date
   722	        fireTimeEndDate = new DateTimeOffset(fireTimeEndDate.DateTime, TimeZoneUtil.GetUtcOffset(fireTimeEndDate.DateTime, TimeZone));
   723	
   724	        // e. Check fireTime against startTime or startTimeOfDay to see which go first.
   725	        DateTimeOffset fireTimeStartDate = startTimeOfDay.GetTimeOfDayForDate(fireTime.Value);
   726	
   727	        // apply the proper offset for the start date
   728	        fireTimeStartDate = new DateTimeOffset(fireTimeStartDate.DateTime, TimeZoneUtil.GetUtcOffset(fireTimeStartDate.DateTime, TimeZone));
   729	
   730	        if (fireTime < fireTimeStartDate)
   731	        {
   732	            return fireTimeStartDate.ToUniversalTime();
   733	        }
   734	
   735	        // f. Continue to calculate the fireTime by incremental unit of intervals.
   736	        // recall that if fireTime was less that fireTimeStartDate, we didn't get this far
   737	        DateTimeOffset startOfDayUtc = TimeZoneUtil.ConvertTime(fireTimeStartDate, TimeZone);
   738	        long secondsAfterStart = (long) (fireTime.Value - startOfDayUtc).TotalSeconds;
   739	        long repeatLong = RepeatInterval;
   740	
   741	        DateTimeOffset sTime = fireTimeStartDate.ToUniversalTime();
   742	        IntervalUnit repeatUnit = RepeatIntervalUnit;
   743	        long jumpCount = 0;
   744	        if (repeatUnit == IntervalUnit.Second)
   745	        {
   746	            jumpCount = secondsAfterStart / repeatLong;
   747	            if (secondsAfterStart % repeatLong != 0)
   748	            {
   749	                jumpCount++;
   750	            }
   751	
   752	            sTime = sTime.AddSeconds(RepeatInterval * (int) jumpCount);
   753	            fireTime = TimeZoneUtil.ConvertTime(sTime, TimeZone);
   754	        }
   755	        else if (repeatUnit == IntervalUnit.Minute)
   756	        {
   757	            jumpCount = secondsAfterStart / (repeatLong * 60L);
   758	            if (secondsAfterStart % (repeatLong * 60L) != 0)
   759	            {
   760	                jumpCount++;
   761	            }
   762	            sTime = sTime.AddMinutes(RepeatInterval * (int) jumpCount);
   763	            fireTime = TimeZoneUtil.ConvertTime(sTime, TimeZone);
   764	        }
   765	        else if (repeatUnit == IntervalUnit.Hour)
   766	        {
   767	            jumpCount = secondsAfterStart / (repeatLong * 60L * 60L);
   768	            if (secondsAfterStart % (repeatLong * 60L * 60L) != 0)
   769	            {
   770	                jumpCount++;
   771	            }
   772	            sTime = sTime.AddHours(RepeatInterval * (int) jumpCount);
   773	            fireTime = TimeZoneUtil.ConvertTime(sTime, TimeZone);
   774	        }
   775	
   776	        // g. Check if we've exceeded the per-day repeat count.
   777	        if (repeatCount != RepeatIndefinitely && jumpCount > repeatCount)
   778	        {
   779	            fireTime = AdvanceToNextDayOfWeekIfNecessary(fireTime.Value, true);
   780	            if (fireTime is null)
   781	            {
   782	                return null;
   783	            }
   784	            fireTime = startTimeOfDay.GetTimeOfDayForDate(fireTime);
   785	            return fireTime?.ToUniversalTime();
   786	        }
   787	
   788	        // h. Ensure this new fireTime is within the day, or else we need to advance to next day.
   789	        if (fireTime > fireTimeEndDate)
   790	        {
   791	            fireTime = AdvanceToNextDayOfWeekIfNecessary(fireTime.Value, IsSameDay(fireTime.Value, fireTimeEndDate));
   792	            // make sure we hit the startTimeOfDay on the new day
   793	            fireTime = startTimeOfDay.GetTimeOfDayForDate(fireTime);
   794	        }
   795	
   796	        // i. Return calculated fireTime.
   797	        return fireTime?.ToUniversalTime();
   798	    }
   799	
   800	    private bool IsSameDay(DateTimeOffset d1, DateTimeOffset d2)
   801	    {
   802	        DateTimeOffset c1 = CreateCalendarTime(d1);
   803	        DateTimeOffset c2 = CreateCalendarTime(d2);
   804	
   805	        return c1.Date == c2.Date;
   806	    }
   807	
   808	    /// <summary>
   809	    /// Given fireTime time determine if it is on a valid day of week. If so, simply return it unaltered,
   810	    /// if not, advance to the next valid week day, and set the time of day to the start time of day.
   811	    /// </summary>
   812	    /// <param name="fireTime">given next fireTime.</param>
   813	    /// <param name="forceToAdvanceNextDay">flag to whether to advance day without check existing week day. This scenario
   814	    /// can happen when a caller determine fireTime has passed the endTimeOfDay that fireTime should move to next day anyway.
   815	    /// </param>
   816	    /// <returns>a next day fireTime.</returns>
   817	    private DateTimeOffset? AdvanceToNextDayOfWeekIfNecessary(DateTimeOffset fireTime, bool forceToAdvanceNextDay)
   818	    {
   819	        // a. Advance or adjust to next dayOfWeek if need to first, starting next day with startTimeOfDay.
   820	        TimeOfDay startTimeOfDay = StartTimeOfDay;
   821	        // Get converted start date based on fireTime; fireTime already has the offset applied
   822	        DateTimeOffset fireTimeStartDate = startTimeOfDay.GetTimeOfDayForDate(fireTime);
   823	        DateTimeOffset fireTimeStartDateCal = fireTimeStartDate;
   824	        DayOfWeek dayOfWeekOfFireTime = fireTimeStartDateCal.DayOfWeek;
   825	
   826	        // b2. We need to advance to another day if isAfterTimePassEndTimeOfDay is true, or dayOfWeek is not set.
   827	        var daysOfWeek = new HashSet<DayOfWeek>(DaysOfWeek);
   828	        if (forceToAdvanceNextDay || !daysOfWeek.Contains(dayOfWeekOfFireTime))
   829	        {
   830	            // Advance one day at a time until next available date.
   831	            for (int i = 1; i <= 7; i++)
   832	            {
   833	                fireTimeStartDateCal = fireTimeStartDateCal.AddDays(1);
   834	                dayOfWeekOfFireTime = fireTimeStartDateCal.DayOfWeek;
   835	                if (daysOfWeek.Contains(dayOfWeekOfFireTime))
   836	                {
   837	                    fireTime = fireTimeStartDateCal;
   838	                    // apply timezone for this date & time
   839	                    fireTime = new DateTimeOffset(fireTime.DateTime, TimeZoneUtil.GetUtcOffset(fireTime, TimeZone));
   840	                    break;
   841	                }
   842	            }
   843	        }
   844	
   845	        // Check fireTime not pass the endTime
   846	        DateTimeOffset? endTime = EndTimeUtc;
   847	
   848	        if (endTime is not null && fireTime > endTime.Value)
   849	        {
   850	            return null;
   851	        }
   852	
   853	        return fireTime;
   854	    }
   855	
   856	    /// <summary>
   857	    /// Returns the final time at which the <see cref="IDailyTimeIntervalTrigger" /> will
   858	    /// fire, if there is no end time set, null will be returned.
   859	    /// </summary>
   860	    /// <remarks>Note that the return time may be in the past.</remarks>

    56	    /// <summary>
    57	    /// TimeZoneInfo.ConvertTime is not supported under mono
    58	    /// </summary>
    59	    /// <param name="dateTimeOffset"></param>
    60	    /// <param name="timeZoneInfo"></param>
    61	    /// <returns></returns>
    62	    public static DateTimeOffset ConvertTime(DateTimeOffset dateTimeOffset, TimeZoneInfo timeZoneInfo)
    63	    {
    64	        return TimeZoneInfo.ConvertTime(dateTimeOffset, timeZoneInfo);
    65	    }
    66	
    67	    /// <summary>
    68	    /// TimeZoneInfo.GetUtcOffset(DateTimeOffset) is not supported under mono
    69	    /// </summary>
    70	    /// <param name="dateTimeOffset"></param>
    71	    /// <param name="timeZoneInfo"></param>
    72	    /// <returns></returns>
    73	    public static TimeSpan GetUtcOffset(DateTimeOffset dateTimeOffset, TimeZoneInfo timeZoneInfo)
    74	    {
    75	        if (QuartzEnvironment.IsRunningOnMono)
    76	        {
    77	            return timeZoneInfo.GetUtcOffset(dateTimeOffset.UtcDateTime);
    78	        }
    79	
    80	        return timeZoneInfo.GetUtcOffset(dateTimeOffset);
    81	    }
    82	
    83	    public static TimeSpan GetUtcOffset(DateTime dateTime, TimeZoneInfo timeZoneInfo)
    84	    {
    85	        // Unlike the default behavior of TimeZoneInfo.GetUtcOffset, it is prefered to choose
    86	        // the DAYLIGHT time when the input is ambiguous, because the daylight instance is the
    87	        // FIRST instance, and time moves in a forward direction.
    88	
    89	        TimeSpan offset = timeZoneInfo.IsAmbiguousTime(dateTime)
    90	            ? timeZoneInfo.GetAmbiguousTimeOffsets(dateTime).Max()
    91	            : timeZoneInfo.GetUtcOffset(dateTime);
    92	
    93	        return offset;
    94	    }
    95	
    96	    /// <summary>
    97	    /// Tries to find time zone with given id, has ability do some fallbacks when necessary.
    98	    /// </summary>
    99	    /// <param name="id">System id of the time zone.</param>
   100	    /// <returns></returns>
   101	    public static TimeZoneInfo FindTimeZoneById(string id)
   102	    {
   103	        TimeZoneInfo? info = null;
   104	        try
   105	        {
   106	            info = TimeZoneInfo.FindSystemTimeZoneById(id);
   107	        }
   108	        catch (TimeZoneNotFoundException ex)
   109	        {
   110	            if (timeZoneIdAliases.TryGetValue(id, out var aliasedId))
   111	            {
   112	                try
   113	                {
   114	                    info = TimeZoneInfo.FindSystemTimeZoneById(aliasedId);
   115	                }
   116	                catch
   117	                {
   118	                    var logger = LogProvider.CreateLogger(nameof(TimeZoneUtil));
   119	                    logger.LogError("Could not find time zone using alias id {AliasId}", aliasedId);
   120	                }
   121	            }
   122	
   123	            if (info is null)
   124	            {
   125	                info = CustomResolver(id);
   126	            }
   127	
   128	            if (info is null)
   129	            {
   130	                // we tried our best
   131	                throw new TimeZoneNotFoundException(
   132	                    $"Could not find time zone with id {id}, consider using Quartz.Plugins.TimeZoneConverter for resolving more time zones ids",
   133	                    ex);
   134	            }
   135	        }
   136	
   137	        return info;
   138	    }

   341	    /// <summary>
   342	    /// The TimeOfDay for this trigger to end firing each day.
   343	    /// </summary>
   344	    /// <param name="timeOfDayUtc"></param>
   345	    /// <returns>the updated DailyTimeIntervalScheduleBuilder</returns>
   346	    public DailyTimeIntervalScheduleBuilder EndingDailyAt(TimeOfDay timeOfDayUtc)
   347	    {
   348	        endTimeOfDayUtc = timeOfDayUtc;
   349	        return this;
   350	    }
   351	
   352	    /// <summary>
   353	    /// Calculate and set the EndTimeOfDay using count, interval and StarTimeOfDay. This means
   354	    /// that these must be set before this method is call.
   355	    /// </summary>
   356	    /// <param name="count"></param>
   357	    /// <returns>the updated DailyTimeIntervalScheduleBuilder</returns>
   358	    public DailyTimeIntervalScheduleBuilder EndingDailyAfterCount(int count)
   359	    {
   360	        if (count <= 0)
   361	        {
   362	            Throw.ArgumentException("Ending daily after count must be a positive number!");
   363	        }
   364	
   365	        if (startTimeOfDayUtc is null)
   366	        {
   367	            Throw.ArgumentException("You must set the StartDailyAt() before calling this EndingDailyAfterCount()!");
   368	        }
   369	
   370	        DateTimeOffset today = timeProvider.GetUtcNow();
   371	        DateTimeOffset startTimeOfDayDate = startTimeOfDayUtc.GetTimeOfDayForDate(today);
   372	        DateTimeOffset tomorrow = startTimeOfDayDate.AddDays(1).UtcDateTime.Date;
   373	
   374	        //apply proper offsets according to timezone
   375	        TimeZoneInfo targetTimeZone = timeZone ?? TimeZoneInfo.Local;
   376	        startTimeOfDayDate = new DateTimeOffset(startTimeOfDayDate.DateTime, TimeZoneUtil.GetUtcOffset(startTimeOfDayDate.DateTime, targetTimeZone));
   377	        tomorrow = new DateTimeOffset(tomorrow.DateTime, TimeZoneUtil.GetUtcOffset(tomorrow.DateTime, targetTimeZone));
   378	
   379	        TimeSpan remainingMillisInDay = tomorrow - startTimeOfDayDate;
   380	        TimeSpan intervalInMillis;
   381	        if (intervalUnit == IntervalUnit.Second)
   382	        {
   383	            intervalInMillis = TimeSpan.FromSeconds(interval);
   384	        }
   385	        else if (intervalUnit == IntervalUnit.Minute)
   386	        {
   387	            intervalInMillis = TimeSpan.FromMinutes(interval);
   388	        }
   389	        else if (intervalUnit == IntervalUnit.Hour)
   390	        {
   391	            intervalInMillis = TimeSpan.FromHours(interval);
   392	        }
   393	        else
   394	        {
   395	            Throw.ArgumentException("The IntervalUnit: " + intervalUnit + " is invalid for this trigger.");
   396	            return this;
   397	        }
   398	
   399	        if (remainingMillisInDay < intervalInMillis)
   400	        {
   401	            Throw.ArgumentException("The startTimeOfDay is too late with given Interval and IntervalUnit values.");
   402	        }
   403	
   404	        long maxNumOfCount = remainingMillisInDay.Ticks / intervalInMillis.Ticks;
   405	        if (count > maxNumOfCount)
   406	        {
   407	            Throw.ArgumentException("The given count " + count + " is too large! The max you can set is " + maxNumOfCount);
   408	        }
   409	
   410	        TimeSpan incrementInMillis = TimeSpan.FromTicks((count - 1) * intervalInMillis.Ticks);
   411	        DateTimeOffset endTimeOfDayDate = startTimeOfDayDate.Add(incrementInMillis);
   412	
   413	        if (endTimeOfDayDate >= tomorrow)
   414	        {
   415	            Throw.ArgumentException("The given count " + count + " is too large! The max you can set is " + maxNumOfCount);
   416	        }
   417	
   418	        DateTime cal = timeProvider.GetUtcNow().Date;
   419	        cal = cal.Add(endTimeOfDayDate.TimeOfDay);
   420	        endTimeOfDayUtc = TimeOfDay.HourMinuteAndSecondOfDay(cal.Hour, cal.Minute, cal.Second);
   421	        return this;
   422	    }

    27	
    28	/// <summary>
    29	/// A <see cref="IScheduleBuilder"/> implementation that build schedule for DailyTimeIntervalTrigger.
    30	/// </summary>
    31	/// <remarks>
    32	/// <para>
    33	/// This builder provide an extra convenient method for you to set the trigger's EndTimeOfDay. You may
    34	/// use either endingDailyAt() or EndingDailyAfterCount() to set the value. The later will auto calculate
    35	/// your EndTimeOfDay by using the interval, IntervalUnit and StartTimeOfDay to perform the calculation.
    36	/// </para>
    37	/// <para>
    38	/// When using EndingDailyAfterCount(), you should note that it is used to calculating EndTimeOfDay. So
    39	/// if your startTime on the first day is already pass by a time that would not add up to the count you
    40	/// expected, until the next day comes. Remember that DailyTimeIntervalTrigger will use StartTimeOfDay
    41	/// and endTimeOfDay as fresh per each day!
    42	/// </para>
    43	/// <para>
    44	/// Quartz provides a builder-style API for constructing scheduling-related
    45	/// entities via a Domain-Specific Language (DSL).  The DSL can best be
    46	/// utilized through the usage of static imports of the methods on the classes
    47	/// <see cref="TriggerBuilder" />, <see cref="JobBuilder" />,
    48	/// <see cref="DateBuilder" />, <see cref="JobKey" />, <see cref="TriggerKey" />
    49	/// and the various <see cref="IScheduleBuilder" /> implementations.
    50	/// </para>
    51	/// <para>Client code can then use the DSL to write code such as this:</para>
    52	/// <code>
    53	///         IJobDetail job = JobBuilder.Create&lt;MyJob>()
    54	///             .WithIdentity("myJob")
    55	///             .Build();
    56	///
    57	///         ITrigger trigger = TriggerBuilder.Create()
    58	///             .WithIdentity(triggerKey("myTrigger", "myTriggerGroup"))
    59	///             .WithDailyTimeIntervalSchedule(x =>
    60	///                        x.WithIntervalInMinutes(15)
    61	///                        .StartingDailyAt(TimeOfDay.HourAndMinuteOfDay(8, 0)))
    62	///             .Build();
    63	///
    64	///         scheduler.scheduleJob(job, trigger);
    65	/// </code>
    66	/// </remarks>
    67	/// <author>James House</author>
    68	/// <author>Zemian Deng saltnlight5@gmail.com</author>
    69	/// <author>Nuno Maia (.NET)</author>
    70	public sealed class DailyTimeIntervalScheduleBuilder : ScheduleBuilder<IDailyTimeIntervalTrigger>
    71	{
    72	    private readonly TimeProvider timeProvider;
    73	
    74	    private int interval = 1;
    75	    private IntervalUnit intervalUnit = IntervalUnit.Minute;
    76	    private HashSet<DayOfWeek>? daysOfWeek;
    77	    private TimeOfDay? startTimeOfDayUtc;
    78	    private TimeOfDay? endTimeOfDayUtc;
    79	    private int repeatCount = DailyTimeIntervalTriggerImpl.RepeatIndefinitely;
    80	    private TimeZoneInfo? timeZone;
    81	
    82	    private int misfireInstruction = MisfireInstruction.SmartPolicy;
    83	
    84	    /// <summary>
    85	    /// A set of all days of the week.
    86	    /// </summary>
    87	    /// <remarks>
    88	    /// The set contains all values between <see cref="DayOfWeek.Sunday"/> and <see cref="DayOfWeek.Saturday"/>
    89	    /// </remarks>
    90	    public static readonly IReadOnlyCollection<DayOfWeek> AllDaysOfTheWeek;
    91	
    92	    /// <summary>
    93	    /// A set of the business days of the week (for locales similar to the USA).
    94	    /// </summary>
    95	    /// <remarks>
    96	    /// The set contains all values between <see cref="DayOfWeek.Monday"/> and <see cref="DayOfWeek.Friday"/>
    97	    /// </remarks>
    98	    public static readonly IReadOnlyCollection<DayOfWeek> MondayThroughFriday;
    99	
   100	    /// <summary>
   101	    /// A set of the weekend days of the week (for locales similar to the USA).
   102	    /// </summary>
   103	    /// <remarks>
   104	    /// The set contains <see cref="DayOfWeek.Saturday"/> and <see cref="DayOfWeek.Sunday"/>
   105	    /// </remarks>
   106	    public static readonly IReadOnlyCollection<DayOfWeek> SaturdayAndSunday;
   107	
   108	    static DailyTimeIntervalScheduleBuilder()
   109	    {
   110	        var allDaysOfTheWeek = new HashSet<DayOfWeek>();
   111	        var mondayThroughFriday = new HashSet<DayOfWeek>();
   112	        foreach (var dayOfWeek in Enum.GetValues<DayOfWeek>())
   113	        {
   114	            allDaysOfTheWeek.Add(dayOfWeek);
   115	
   116	            if (dayOfWeek >= DayOfWeek.Monday && dayOfWeek <= DayOfWeek.Friday)
   117	            {
   118	                mondayThroughFriday.Add(dayOfWeek);
   119	            }
   120	        }
   121	
   122	        SaturdayAndSunday = new HashSet<DayOfWeek>
   123	        {
   124	            DayOfWeek.Sunday,
   125	            DayOfWeek.Saturday
   126	        };
   127	
   128	        AllDaysOfTheWeek = allDaysOfTheWeek;
   129	        MondayThroughFriday = mondayThroughFriday;
   130	        AllDaysOfTheWeek = new HashSet<DayOfWeek>(AllDaysOfTheWeek);

   144	    /// <returns>The new DailyTimeIntervalScheduleBuilder</returns>
   145	    public static DailyTimeIntervalScheduleBuilder Create(TimeProvider? timeProvider = null)
   146	    {
   147	        return new DailyTimeIntervalScheduleBuilder(timeProvider ?? TimeProvider.System);
   148	    }
   149	
   150	    /// <summary>
   151	    /// Build the actual Trigger -- NOT intended to be invoked by end users,
   152	    /// but will rather be invoked by a TriggerBuilder which this
   153	    /// ScheduleBuilder is given to.
   154	    /// </summary>
   155	    /// <returns></returns>
   156	    public override IMutableTrigger Build()
   157	    {
   158	        DailyTimeIntervalTriggerImpl st = new DailyTimeIntervalTriggerImpl();
   159	        st.RepeatInterval = interval;
   160	        st.RepeatIntervalUnit = intervalUnit;
   161	        st.MisfireInstruction = misfireInstruction;
   162	        st.RepeatCount = repeatCount;
   163	        st.timeZone = timeZone;
   164	
   165	        if (daysOfWeek is not null)
   166	        {
   167	            st.DaysOfWeek = new HashSet<DayOfWeek>(daysOfWeek);
   168	        }
   169	        else
   170	        {
   171	            st.DaysOfWeek = new HashSet<DayOfWeek>(AllDaysOfTheWeek);
   172	        }
   173	
   174	        if (startTimeOfDayUtc is not null)
   175	        {
   176	            st.StartTimeOfDay = startTimeOfDayUtc;
   177	        }
   178	        else
   179	        {
   180	            st.StartTimeOfDay = TimeOfDay.HourAndMinuteOfDay(0, 0);
   181	        }
   182	
   183	        if (endTimeOfDayUtc is not null)
   184	        {
   185	            st.EndTimeOfDay = endTimeOfDayUtc;
   186	        }
   187	        else
   188	        {
   189	            st.EndTimeOfDay = TimeOfDay.HourMinuteAndSecondOfDay(23, 59, 59);
   190	        }
   191	
   192	        return st;
   193	    }
   194

   203	    /// <seealso cref="ICalendarIntervalTrigger.RepeatInterval" />
   204	    /// <seealso cref="ICalendarIntervalTrigger.RepeatIntervalUnit" />
   205	    public DailyTimeIntervalScheduleBuilder WithInterval(int interval, IntervalUnit unit)
   206	    {
   207	        if (!(unit == IntervalUnit.Second ||
   208	              unit == IntervalUnit.Minute || unit == IntervalUnit.Hour))
   209	        {
   210	            Throw.ArgumentException("Invalid repeat IntervalUnit (must be Second, Minute or Hour).");
   211	        }
   212	
   213	        ValidateInterval(interval);
   214	        this.interval = interval;
   215	        intervalUnit = unit;
   216	        return this;
   217	    }

   226	    /// <see cref="IDailyTimeIntervalTrigger.RepeatIntervalUnit"/>
   227	    public DailyTimeIntervalScheduleBuilder WithIntervalInSeconds(int intervalInSeconds)

using Quartz;
using Quartz.Spi;

DateTime startDateTime = new DateTime(2020, 10, 25);
DateTimeOffset startDateTimeOffset = new DateTimeOffset(startDateTime);
int daysAhead = 3;

TriggerBuilder triggerBuilder = TriggerBuilder.Create()
    .WithIdentity("id")
    .ForJob("job")
    .StartAt(new DateTimeOffset(startDateTime.AddMinutes(1).AddSeconds(5)))
    .WithDailyTimeIntervalSchedule(
        scheduleBuilder =>
        {
            scheduleBuilder.OnEveryDay().WithIntervalInHours(24);
            scheduleBuilder
                .StartingDailyAt(new TimeOfDay(0, 1, 5))
                .EndingDailyAt(new TimeOfDay(23, 59, 59))
                .WithMisfireHandlingInstructionDoNothing();
        });

IReadOnlyList<DateTimeOffset> fireTimes =
    TriggerUtils.ComputeFireTimesBetween((IOperableTrigger) triggerBuilder.Build(), null,
        startDateTimeOffset,
        startDateTimeOffset.AddDays(daysAhead));

Console.WriteLine($"Local TZ: {TimeZoneInfo.Local.Id} {TimeZoneInfo.Local.DisplayName}");
Console.WriteLine($"from {startDateTimeOffset:o} to {startDateTimeOffset.AddDays(daysAhead):o}");
Console.WriteLine($"count {fireTimes.Count}");
foreach (var ft in fireTimes)
{
    Console.WriteLine($"{ft:o} local={ft.LocalDateTime:O} offset={ft.Offset}");
}
if (fireTimes.Count != 3 || fireTimes.Select(x => x.LocalDateTime).ToArray() is var l &&
    (l[0] != new DateTime(2020,10,25,0,1,5) || l[1] != new DateTime(2020,10,26,0,1,5) || l[2] != new DateTime(2020,10,27,0,1,5)))
{
    Environment.ExitCode = 1;
}

cat > /tmp/reproquartz/Program.cs <<'EOF'
using System;
using System.Collections.Generic;
using System.Linq;
using Quartz;
using Quartz.Spi;

DateTime startDateTime = new DateTime(2020, 10, 25);
DateTimeOffset startDateTimeOffset = new DateTimeOffset(startDateTime);
int daysAhead = 3;

TriggerBuilder triggerBuilder = TriggerBuilder.Create()
    .WithIdentity("id")
    .ForJob("job")
    .StartAt(new DateTimeOffset(startDateTime.AddMinutes(1).AddSeconds(5)))
    .WithDailyTimeIntervalSchedule(
        scheduleBuilder =>
        {
            scheduleBuilder.OnEveryDay().WithIntervalInHours(24);
            scheduleBuilder
                .StartingDailyAt(new TimeOfDay(0, 1, 5))
                .EndingDailyAt(new TimeOfDay(23, 59, 59))
                .WithMisfireHandlingInstructionDoNothing();
        });

IReadOnlyList<DateTimeOffset> fireTimes =
    TriggerUtils.ComputeFireTimesBetween((IOperableTrigger) triggerBuilder.Build(), null,
        startDateTimeOffset,
        startDateTimeOffset.AddDays(daysAhead));

Console.WriteLine($"Local TZ: {TimeZoneInfo.Local.Id} {TimeZoneInfo.Local.DisplayName}");
Console.WriteLine($"from {startDateTimeOffset:o} to {startDateTimeOffset.AddDays(daysAhead):o}");
Console.WriteLine($"count {fireTimes.Count}");
foreach (var ft in fireTimes)
{
    Console.WriteLine($"{ft:o} local={ft.LocalDateTime:O} offset={ft.Offset}");
}
var l = fireTimes.Select(x => x.LocalDateTime).ToArray();
if (fireTimes.Count != 3 || l[0] != new DateTime(2020,10,25,0,1,5) || l[1] != new DateTime(2020,10,26,0,1,5) || l[2] != new DateTime(2020,10,27,0,1,5))
{
    Environment.ExitCode = 1;
}
EOF

   390	    protected override bool ValidateMisfireInstruction(int misfireInstruction)
   391	    {
   392	        if (misfireInstruction < Quartz.MisfireInstruction.IgnoreMisfirePolicy)
   393	        {
   394	            return false;
   395	        }
   396	        if (misfireInstruction > Quartz.MisfireInstruction.DailyTimeIntervalTrigger.DoNothing)

   404	    /// <summary>
   405	    /// Updates the <see cref="ICalendarIntervalTrigger" />'s state based on the
   406	    /// MisfireInstruction.XXX that was selected when the <see cref="IDailyTimeIntervalTrigger" />
   407	    /// was created.
   408	    /// </summary>
   409	    /// <remarks>
   410	    /// If the misfire instruction is set to <see cref="MisfireInstruction.SmartPolicy" />,
   411	    /// then the following scheme will be used:
   412	    /// <ul>
   413	    ///     <li>The instruction will be interpreted as <see cref="MisfireInstruction.DailyTimeIntervalTrigger.FireOnceNow" /></li>
   414	    /// </ul>
   415	    /// </remarks>
   416	    public override void UpdateAfterMisfire(ICalendar? cal)
   417	    {
   418	        int instr = MisfireInstruction;
   419	
   420	        if (instr == Quartz.MisfireInstruction.IgnoreMisfirePolicy)
   421	        {
   422	            return;
   423	        }
   424	
   425	        if (instr == Quartz.MisfireInstruction.SmartPolicy)
   426	        {
   427	            instr = Quartz.MisfireInstruction.DailyTimeIntervalTrigger.FireOnceNow;
   428	        }
   429	
   430	        if (instr == Quartz.MisfireInstruction.DailyTimeIntervalTrigger.DoNothing)
   431	        {
   432	            DateTimeOffset? newFireTime = GetFireTimeAfter(TimeProvider.GetUtcNow());
   433	            while (newFireTime is not null && cal is not null && !cal.IsTimeIncluded(newFireTime.Value))
   434	            {
   435	                newFireTime = GetFireTimeAfter(newFireTime);
   436	            }
   437	            SetNextFireTimeUtc(newFireTime);
   438	        }
   439	        else if (instr == Quartz.MisfireInstruction.DailyTimeIntervalTrigger.FireOnceNow)
   440	        {
   441	            // fire once now...
   442	            SetNextFireTimeUtc(TimeProvider.GetUtcNow());
   443	            // the new fire time afterward will magically preserve the original
   444	            // time of day for firing for day/week/month interval triggers,
   445	            // because of the way getFireTimeAfter() works - in its always restarting
   446	            // computation from the start time.
   447	        }
   448	    }
   449	
   450	    internal override void UpdateAfterMisfire(ICalendar? cal, TimeSpan misfireThreshold)
   451	    {
   452	        int instr = MisfireInstruction;
   453	
   454	        if (instr == Quartz.MisfireInstruction.IgnoreMisfirePolicy)
   455	        {
   456	            return;
   457	        }
   458	
   459	        if (instr == Quartz.MisfireInstruction.SmartPolicy)
   460	        {
   461	            instr = Quartz.MisfireInstruction.DailyTimeIntervalTrigger.FireOnceNow;
   462	        }
   463	
   464	        if (instr == Quartz.MisfireInstruction.DailyTimeIntervalTrigger.DoNothing)
   465	        {
   466	            DateTimeOffset? newFireTime = GetFireTimeAfter(TimeProvider.GetUtcNow() - misfireThreshold);
   467	            while (newFireTime != null && cal != null && !cal.IsTimeIncluded(newFireTime.Value))
   468	            {
   469	                newFireTime = GetFireTimeAfter(newFireTime);
   470	            }
   471	            SetNextFireTimeUtc(newFireTime);
   472	        }
   473	        else if (instr == Quartz.MisfireInstruction.DailyTimeIntervalTrigger.FireOnceNow)
   474	        {
   475	            SetNextFireTimeUtc(TimeProvider.GetUtcNow());
   476	        }
   477	    }

  1180	    /// <summary>
  1181	    /// Regression test for https://github.com/quartznet/quartznet/issues/859
  1182	    /// GetFireTimeAfter should not mutate the trigger's StartTimeUtc field.
  1183	    /// </summary>
  1184	    [Test]
  1185	    public void GetFireTimeAfterShouldNotMutateStartTimeUtc()
  1186	    {
  1187	        DateTimeOffset originalStartTime = DateBuilder.DateOf(0, 0, 0, 1, 1, 2024);
  1188	        var trigger = new DailyTimeIntervalTriggerImpl
  1189	        {
  1190	            StartTimeUtc = originalStartTime,
  1191	            StartTimeOfDay = new TimeOfDay(8, 0, 0),
  1192	            EndTimeOfDay = new TimeOfDay(17, 0, 0),
  1193	            RepeatIntervalUnit = IntervalUnit.Hour,
  1194	            RepeatInterval = 1
  1195	        };
  1196	
  1197	        // Call with a time after the daily start time to exercise the code path
  1198	        // that previously mutated startTimeUtc
  1199	        DateTimeOffset afterTime = DateBuilder.DateOf(10, 0, 0, 1, 1, 2024);
  1200	        trigger.GetFireTimeAfter(afterTime);
  1201	
  1202	        Assert.That(trigger.StartTimeUtc, Is.EqualTo(originalStartTime),
  1203	            "StartTimeUtc should not be modified by GetFireTimeAfter");
  1204	
  1205	        // Also verify ComputeFirstFireTimeUtc doesn't mutate it
  1206	        trigger.StartTimeUtc = originalStartTime;
  1207	        trigger.ComputeFirstFireTimeUtc(null);
  1208	
  1209	        Assert.That(trigger.StartTimeUtc, Is.EqualTo(originalStartTime),
  1210	            "StartTimeUtc should not be modified by ComputeFirstFireTimeUtc");
  1211	    }

    22	namespace Quartz;
    23	
    24	/// <summary>
    25	/// Represents a time in hour, minute and second of any given day.
    26	/// <remarks>
    27	/// <para>
    28	/// The hour is in 24-hour convention, meaning values are from 0 to 23.
    29	/// </para>
    30	/// </remarks>
    31	/// </summary>
    32	/// <seealso cref="IDailyTimeIntervalTrigger"/>
    33	/// <author>James House</author>
    34	/// <author>Zemian Deng saltnlight5@gmail.com</author>
    35	/// <author>Nuno Maia (.NET)</author>
    36	[Serializable]
    37	public sealed class TimeOfDay
    38	{
    39	    /// <summary>
    40	    /// Create a TimeOfDay instance for the given hour, minute and second.
    41	    /// </summary>
    42	    /// <param name="hour">The hour of day, between 0 and 23.</param>
    43	    /// <param name="minute">The minute of the hour, between 0 and 59.</param>
    44	    /// <param name="second">The second of the minute, between 0 and 59.</param>
    45	    public TimeOfDay(int hour, int minute, int second)
    46	    {
    47	        Hour = hour;
    48	        Minute = minute;
    49	        Second = second;
    50	        Validate();
    51	    }
    52	
    53	    /// <summary>
    54	    /// Create a TimeOfDay instance for the given hour, minute (at the zero second of the minute).
    55	    /// </summary>
    56	    /// <param name="hour">The hour of day, between 0 and 23.</param>
    57	    /// <param name="minute">The minute of the hour, between 0 and 59.</param>
    58	    public TimeOfDay(int hour, int minute)
    59	    {
    60	        Hour = hour;
    61	        Minute = minute;
    62	        Second = 0;
    63	        Validate();
    64	    }
    65	
    66	    private void Validate()
    67	    {
    68	        if (Hour < 0 || Hour > 23)
    69	        {
    70	            Throw.ArgumentException("Hour must be from 0 to 23");
    71	        }
    72	
    73	        if (Minute < 0 || Minute > 59)
    74	        {
    75	            Throw.ArgumentException("Minute must be from 0 to 59");
    76	        }
    77	
    78	        if (Second < 0 || Second > 59)
    79	        {
    80	            Throw.ArgumentException("Second must be from 0 to 59");
    81	        }
    82	    }
    83	
    84	    /// <summary>
    85	    /// Create a TimeOfDay instance for the given hour, minute and second.
    86	    /// </summary>
    87	    /// <param name="hour">The hour of day, between 0 and 23.</param>
    88	    /// <param name="minute">The minute of the hour, between 0 and 59.</param>
    89	    /// <param name="second">The second of the minute, between 0 and 59.</param>
    90	    /// <returns></returns>
    91	    public static TimeOfDay HourMinuteAndSecondOfDay(int hour, int minute, int second)
    92	    {
    93	        return new TimeOfDay(hour, minute, second);
    94	    }
    95	
    96	    /// <summary>
    97	    /// Create a TimeOfDay instance for the given hour, minute (at the zero second of the minute)..
    98	    /// </summary>
    99	    /// <param name="hour">The hour of day, between 0 and 23.</param>
   100	    /// <param name="minute">The minute of the hour, between 0 and 59.</param>
   101	    /// <returns>The newly instantiated TimeOfDay</returns>
   102	    public static TimeOfDay HourAndMinuteOfDay(int hour, int minute)
   103	    {
   104	        return new TimeOfDay(hour, minute);
   105	    }
   106	
   107	    /// <summary>
   108	    /// The hour of the day (between 0 and 23).
   109	    /// </summary>
   110	    public int Hour { get; }
   111	
   112	    /// <summary>
   113	    /// The minute of the hour (between 0 and 59).
   114	    /// </summary>
   115	    public int Minute { get; }
   116	
   117	    /// <summary>
   118	    /// The second of the minute (between 0 and 59).
   119	    /// </summary>
   120	    public int Second { get; }
   121	
   122	    /// <summary>
   123	    /// Determine with this time of day is before the given time of day.
   124	    /// </summary>
   125	    /// <param name="timeOfDay"></param>
   126	    /// <returns>True this time of day is before the given time of day.</returns>
   127	    public bool Before(TimeOfDay timeOfDay)
   128	    {
   129	        if (timeOfDay.Hour > Hour)
   130	        {
   131	            return true;
   132	        }
   133	        if (timeOfDay.Hour < Hour)
   134	        {
   135	            return false;
   136	        }
   137	
   138	        if (timeOfDay.Minute > Minute)
   139	        {
   140	            return true;
   141	        }
   142	        if (timeOfDay.Minute < Minute)
   143	        {
   144	            return false;
   145	        }
   146	
   147	        if (timeOfDay.Second > Second)
   148	        {
   149	            return true;
   150	        }
   151	        if (timeOfDay.Second < Second)
   152	        {
   153	            return false;
   154	        }
   155	
   156	        return false; // must be equal...
   157	    }
   158	
   159	    public override bool Equals(object? obj)
   160	    {
   161	        if (obj is not TimeOfDay timeOfDay)
   162	        {
   163	            return false;
   164	        }
   165	
   166	        return timeOfDay.Hour == Hour && timeOfDay.Minute == Minute && timeOfDay.Second == Second;
   167	    }
   168	
   169	    public override int GetHashCode()
   170	    {
   171	        return (Hour + 1) ^ (Minute + 1) ^ (Second + 1);
   172	    }
   173	
   174	    /// <summary>
   175	    /// Return a date with time of day reset to this object values. The millisecond value will be zero.
   176	    /// </summary>
   177	    /// <param name="dateTime"></param>
   178	    public DateTimeOffset? GetTimeOfDayForDate(DateTimeOffset? dateTime)
   179	    {
   180	        if (dateTime is null)
   181	        {
   182	            return null;
   183	        }
   184	
   185	        return GetTimeOfDayForDate(dateTime.Value);
   186	    }
   187	
   188	    /// <summary>
   189	    /// Return a date with time of day reset to this object values. The millisecond value will be zero.
   190	    /// </summary>
   191	    /// <param name="dateTime"></param>
   192	    public DateTimeOffset GetTimeOfDayForDate(DateTimeOffset dateTime)
   193	    {
   194	        DateTimeOffset cal = new DateTimeOffset(dateTime.Date, dateTime.Offset);
   195	        TimeSpan t = new TimeSpan(0, Hour, Minute, Second);
   196	        return cal.Add(t);
   197	    }
   198	
   199	    public override string ToString()
   200	    {
   201	        return "TimeOfDay[" + Hour + ":" + Minute + ":" + Second + "]";
   202	    }
   203	}

   842	
   843	        // CRITICAL: Ensure we never return a time <= the original input.
   844	        // This prevents infinite loops during DST transitions where DST adjustment logic
   845	        // might inadvertently return the same time we were given.
   846	        // This is especially important during spring-forward transitions where scheduled times
   847	        // don't exist (e.g., 2:01 AM when clocks jump from 2:00 AM to 3:00 AM).
   848	        if (originalAfterTime != null && time != null && time <= originalAfterTime)

   850	            // The calculated time is not progressing forward. This can happen during DST transitions
   851	            // when PreserveHourOfDayAcrossDaylightSavings is true and the adjustment logic
   852	            // brings us back to the same time.
   853	
   854	            // To fix this, we skip forward past the problematic DST window by advancing the
   855	            // reference time by a couple of hours and then recursively calling GetFireTimeAfter.
   856	            // The recursive call re-runs the same timezone/DST adjustment logic, but starting from
   857	            // a point safely beyond the transition, which guarantees forward progress.
   858	            DateTimeOffset skipAhead = originalAfterTime.Value.AddHours(2); // Skip past DST transition
   859	            return GetFireTimeAfter(skipAhead, ignoreEndTime, recursionDepth + 1);
   860	        }
   861	
   862	        return time;

   864	
   865	    private bool DaylightSavingHourShiftOccurredAndAdvanceNeeded(ref DateTimeOffset newTime, int initialHourOfDay)
   866	    {
   867	        //need to apply timezone again to properly check if initialHourOfDay has changed.
   868	        DateTimeOffset toCheck = TimeZoneUtil.ConvertTime(newTime, TimeZone);
   869	
   870	        if (PreserveHourOfDayAcrossDaylightSavings && toCheck.Hour != initialHourOfDay)
   871	        {
   872	            //first apply the date, and then find the proper timezone offset
   873	            newTime = new DateTimeOffset(newTime.Year, newTime.Month, newTime.Day, initialHourOfDay, newTime.Minute, newTime.Second, newTime.Millisecond, TimeSpan.Zero);
   874	            newTime = new DateTimeOffset(newTime.DateTime, TimeZoneUtil.GetUtcOffset(newTime.DateTime, TimeZone));
   875	
   876	            //TimeZone.IsInvalidTime is true, if this hour does not exist in the specified timezone
   877	            bool isInvalid = TimeZone.IsInvalidTime(newTime.DateTime);
   878	
   879	            if (isInvalid && SkipDayIfHourDoesNotExist)
   880	            {
   881	                return SkipDayIfHourDoesNotExist;
   882	            }
   883	            //don't skip this day, instead find closest valid time by adding minutes.
   884	            while (TimeZone.IsInvalidTime(newTime.DateTime))
   885	            {
   886	                newTime = newTime.AddMinutes(1);
   887	            }
   888	
   889	            //apply proper offset for the adjusted time
   890	            newTime = new DateTimeOffset(newTime.DateTime, TimeZoneUtil.GetUtcOffset(newTime.DateTime, TimeZone));
   891	        }
   892	        return false;
   893	    }
   894	
   895	    private void MakeHourAdjustmentIfNeeded(ref DateTimeOffset sTime, int initialHourOfDay)
   896	    {
   897	        //this method was made to adjust the time if a DST occurred, this is to stay consistent with the time
   898	        //we are checking against, which is the afterTime. There were problems the occurred when the DST adjustment
   899	        //took the time an hour back, leading to the times were not being adjusted properly.
   900	
   901	        //avoid shifts in day, otherwise this will cause an infinite loop in the code.
   902	        int initalYear = sTime.Year;
   903	        int initalMonth = sTime.Month;
   904	        int initialDay = sTime.Day;
   905	
   906	        sTime = TimeZoneUtil.ConvertTime(sTime, TimeZone);
   907	
   908	        if (PreserveHourOfDayAcrossDaylightSavings && sTime.Hour != initialHourOfDay)
   909	        {
   910	            //first apply the date, and then find the proper timezone offset
   911	            sTime = new DateTimeOffset(initalYear, initalMonth, initialDay, initialHourOfDay, sTime.Minute, sTime.Second, sTime.Millisecond, TimeSpan.Zero);
   912	            sTime = new DateTimeOffset(sTime.DateTime, TimeZoneUtil.GetUtcOffset(sTime.DateTime, TimeZone));
   913	        }
   914	    }

   740	
   741	        DateTimeOffset sTime = fireTimeStartDate.ToUniversalTime();

   748	            {
   749	                jumpCount++;
   750	            }
   751

using System;
using System.Collections.Generic;
using Quartz;
using Quartz.Spi;

foreach (var startDateTime in new[] { new DateTime(2020, 3, 29), new DateTime(2020, 10, 25) })
{
    DateTimeOffset startDateTimeOffset = new DateTimeOffset(startDateTime);
    var triggerBuilder = TriggerBuilder.Create()
        .StartAt(new DateTimeOffset(startDateTime.AddMinutes(1).AddSeconds(5)))
        .WithDailyTimeIntervalSchedule(s => s.OnEveryDay().WithIntervalInHours(24)
            .StartingDailyAt(new TimeOfDay(0, 1, 5))
            .EndingDailyAt(new TimeOfDay(23, 59, 59)));
    var fireTimes = TriggerUtils.ComputeFireTimesBetween((IOperableTrigger)triggerBuilder.Build(), null, startDateTimeOffset, startDateTimeOffset.AddDays(3));
    Console.WriteLine($"Start {startDateTime:d} count {fireTimes.Count}");
    foreach (var ft in fireTimes) Console.WriteLine($"{ft:o} local={ft.LocalDateTime:O}");
}
EOF

   728	
   729	        // e. Check fireTime against startTime or startTimeOfDay to see which go first.
   730	        DateTimeOffset fireTimeStartDate = startTimeOfDay.GetTimeOfDayForDate(fireTime.Value);
   731	
   732	        // apply the proper offset for the start date
   733	        fireTimeStartDate = new DateTimeOffset(fireTimeStartDate.DateTime, TimeZoneUtil.GetUtcOffset(fireTimeStartDate.DateTime, TimeZone));
   734	
   735	        if (fireTime < fireTimeStartDate)
   736	        {
   737	            return fireTimeStartDate.ToUniversalTime();
   738	        }
   739	
   740	        // f. Continue to calculate the fireTime by incremental unit of intervals.
   741	        // recall that if fireTime was less that fireTimeStartDate, we didn't get this far
   742	        long secondsAfterStart = (long) (fireTime.Value.DateTime - fireTimeStartDate.DateTime).TotalSeconds;
   743	        long repeatLong = RepeatInterval;
   744	
   745	        DateTimeOffset sTime = fireTimeStartDate;
   746	        IntervalUnit repeatUnit = RepeatIntervalUnit;
   747	        long jumpCount = 0;
   748	        if (repeatUnit == IntervalUnit.Second)
   749	        {
   750	            jumpCount = secondsAfterStart / repeatLong;
   751	            if (secondsAfterStart % repeatLong != 0)
   752	            {
   753	                jumpCount++;
   754	            }
   755	
   756	            sTime = GetTimeOfDayForDate(sTime.DateTime.AddSeconds(RepeatInterval * (int) jumpCount));
   757	            fireTime = sTime;
   758	        }
   759	        else if (repeatUnit == IntervalUnit.Minute)
   760	        {
   761	            jumpCount = secondsAfterStart / (repeatLong * 60L);
   762	            if (secondsAfterStart % (repeatLong * 60L) != 0)
   763	            {
   764	                jumpCount++;
   765	            }
   766	            sTime = GetTimeOfDayForDate(sTime.DateTime.AddMinutes(RepeatInterval * (int) jumpCount));
   767	            fireTime = sTime;
   768	        }
   769	        else if (repeatUnit == IntervalUnit.Hour)
   770	        {
   771	            jumpCount = secondsAfterStart / (repeatLong * 60L * 60L);
   772	            if (secondsAfterStart % (repeatLong * 60L * 60L) != 0)
   773	            {
   774	                jumpCount++;
   775	            }
   776	            sTime = GetTimeOfDayForDate(sTime.DateTime.AddHours(RepeatInterval * (int) jumpCount));
   777	            fireTime = sTime;
   778	        }
   779	
   780	        // g. Check if we've exceeded the per-day repeat count.
   781	        if (repeatCount != RepeatIndefinitely && jumpCount > repeatCount)
   782	        {
   783	            fireTime = AdvanceToNextDayOfWeekIfNecessary(fireTime.Value, true);
   784	            if (fireTime is null)
   785	            {
   786	                return null;
   787	            }
   788	            fireTime = startTimeOfDay.GetTimeOfDayForDate(fireTime);
   789	            return fireTime?.ToUniversalTime();
   790	        }
   791	
   792	        // h. Ensure this new fireTime is within the day, or else we need to advance to next day.
   793	        if (fireTime > fireTimeEndDate)
   794	        {
   795	            fireTime = AdvanceToNextDayOfWeekIfNecessary(fireTime.Value, IsSameDay(fireTime.Value, fireTimeEndDate));
   796	            // make sure we hit the startTimeOfDay on the new day
   797	            fireTime = startTimeOfDay.GetTimeOfDayForDate(fireTime);
   798	        }
   799	
   800	        // i. Return calculated fireTime.
   801	        return fireTime?.ToUniversalTime();
   802	    }

#!/usr/bin/env python3

import argparse
from pathlib import Path
import subprocess
import sys
import os
import io

from registry import registry


def main() -> None:
    parser = argparse.ArgumentParser(description="Submit changes for review")
    parser.add_argument("-f", "--force", action="store_true", help="Force submit without review")
    args = parser.parse_args()

    repo_root = registry.get("ROOT", os.getenv("ROOT"))
    assert repo_root

    patch_path = Path("/root/model.patch")

    subprocess.run(
        f"git add -A && git diff --cached > {patch_path}",
        shell=True,
        stdout=subprocess.DEVNULL,
        stderr=subprocess.DEVNULL,
        cwd=repo_root,
    )

    patch = patch_path.read_text(errors="backslashreplace")

    submit_review_messages = registry.get("SUBMIT_REVIEW_MESSAGES", [])
    n_stages = len(submit_review_messages)
    current_stage = registry.get("SUBMIT_STAGE", 0)
    if not args.force and current_stage != n_stages:
        message = submit_review_messages[current_stage]
        message = message.replace("{{diff}}", patch)
        message = message.replace("{{problem_statement}}", registry.get("PROBLEM_STATEMENT", ""))
        registry["SUBMIT_STAGE"] = current_stage + 1
        print(message)
        sys.exit(0)

    print("<<SWE_AGENT_SUBMISSION>>")
    print(patch)
    print("<<SWE_AGENT_SUBMISSION>>")
